ANNEXAnnex I 1 Points of view expressed by the carriers and the users interested in combined carriageAnnex II : Statistics (table 1 to 4) 1 .INTRODUCTION2 .1.1. In its directive of 17 February 1975 the Council laid down common rules for certain types of combined rail / road carriage of goods between Member States for a limited period until 31 December 1978. These rules provided especially for the freeing of this type of carriage from any quantitative restriction ( quota ) and the removal ofvarious administrative constraints ( authorizations ) at the latest by 1 October 1975 .Article 7, 1st sub-para, of the Directive lays down that the Commission shall report on the application of the directive and submit proposals relating to it to the Council before 31 December 1977.In accordance with sub-para. 2 of Article 7, which limits the validity of the directive to 31 December 1978, the Council, upon the Commission's proposal, should give a ruling before this date, on the system to be applied subsequently.1.2. The objective of this report is to meet the terms of reference given to the Commission in the 1st sub-para, of Article 7 of the directive. Consequently, in the first instance, it provides information on the application of this directive during the period from 1 October 1975 until 1 July 1977.ENFORCEMENT OF THE DIRECTIVE2.1 .Application measures taken by the Member States2.1.1. In accordance with the provisions of Article 5 of the directive of 17 February 1975 the Member States were obligedto take the necessary measures for the implementation of this directive and to send details of them to the Commission, before 30 June 1975* Q*1 10 February 1976f "the latter sent them to all the Member States for information .To sum up the position, it can be stated that all the Member States tried to meet the common fixed compulsory objectives by appropriate and effective measures. The existence of certain problems, as set out below in Chapter 4, does not affect this general positive impression.Importance, development and distribution of the traffic2.2.1 . General considerationsWithin the framework of this directive, the current experience analyzed in this report covers a period of less than two years up till now. In addition, during the period under consideration, international trade - which since 1950 and2.2.-2- Gross Tonnes Indi ces2981 3668 4452 4664 4301 100 123 149 156 144- 3 --urvril the beginning of the 1970' s had been developing in a continuous fashion at an average rate of nearly 7% p. a . - obviously suffered from the effects of the economic recession and the development of transport carried out by combined techniques was temporarily checked .Consequent ly , the data concerning the development of combined rail/road traffic should be considered in the light of this situation .2.2.2. Development of the traffic - analysis of the figuresOn the basis of the statistics provided by the various combined transport companies , the attached table ( Annex II , Table 1) gives an outline of the development of rail/road traffic carried out by semi-trailers (including vehicle combinations ) as well as swop bodies .Despite taking precautions some double counting hasnot been entirely eliminated. With this reservation one can note that the overall gross traffic (national and international) has developed as follows :Iin 1000 tonnes1972 1973 1974 19751971 iI1976(1 )5332 179The share of international traffic in these figures was about 1 million tonnes in 1976, i.e. _+ 19% of the total traffic .When examining these figures one can see that afterthe decline in 1975 in relation to 1974 the overall traffic for 1976 showed a marked increase .In order to put the combined rail/road carriage in relation to total freight traffic into perspective, it would be wrong to compare the two overall figures. In fact, in so doing, one would come to the false conclusion that combined carriage traffic still plays a rather unimportant role (2).(1) 1977 figures not yet available at the time of compiling this report(2) Example : in 1975, 0.5% of the overall rail freight traffic of the Community -4-This method does not give an exact idea of the situation because it does not compare like with like .Indeed, in this case, no account is taken of the fact that combined rail / road carriage can only be carried out in a rational and profitable way over relatively large distances,over transport links which are fixed in relation to the volume carried and for certain categories of goods. An attempt to draw a comparison on this basis, even though difficult inthe absence of objective criteria, does confirm the factthat in certain sub-markets combined carriage already at present occupies a non-negligible share and this is increasing.But this technique will always face certain limits to its development resulting mainly from the fact that it requires the carriage of very important deadweight ( lorry or semi-trailer). Only the swop-bodies, which resemble a container, avoid this inconvenience.Nevertheless , international traffic carried out by the combined transport companies inside the Community seemsto be developing strongly (+ 22% during the first half of 1977).2.2.3. Contribution of the various commercial combined transport companies to this trafficCombined carriage , which links rail and road transport , and which is called "ferroutage" (road/rail), is carried out through commercial companies with subsidiaries in severalEuropeancountries .- In Germany the KOMBIVERKEHR Company was responsible for 20% of the international traffic in 1975,- In Belgium, the T.R.W. Company was responsible for 9% of this traffic/- in France the NOVATRANS Company was responsible for 40% of this traffic,- In Italy the FERPAC Company was responsible for 2% of this traffic,- In the Netherlands the TRAILSTAR Company was responsible for 10% of this traffic,- In Switzerland the HUPAC Company was responsible for 15% of this traffic .Since 1970 these six companies have been joined by a seventh, the A.S.G. Company (Sweden) in the "Union Inter- nationale des Transports combines rail/route" (U.I.R.R.). In addition a joint rail/road committee has been set UP.» wich the aim of co-ordinating efforts at an international level for thedevelopment of rail/road carriage. The Committee is madeup of the member companies of the U.I.R.R. and the railways of Member States and of Switzerland and Austria.2.2.4. Distribution of traffic by transport linkTable 2 (Annex II) shows the main internationaltransport links concerned in this traffic. Of the 76 links29 concern Italy and, outside the Community, one can especiall note the connections with Spain and with Switzerland.2.2.5. Number of wagons assigned to combined carriageTable 3 (Annex II) shows the number of wagons assigned to combined carriage at the end of 1976, by major categories. Of a total of 2,300 wagons 25% are assignedto international traffic. Nearly 1,100 wagons belong to the German railways and in France nearly 800 wagons belong to the management companies of private wagons.2.2.6. Distribution by nature of combined carriageThe commercial combined carriage comoanies use different "ferroutage" techniques. One can ma!-.<? out two main categories :- techniques where the wagon is adapted to the road vehicle (dropped-axle wagons or wagons with guide raiIs)- techniques where the road vehicle is planned for adaptation to the rail wagon (special semi-trailer or swop-body).It has not been possible to give a distribution of traffic by technique employed. One can only point out that in France, the N0VATRANS Company for the most part uses thekind of dropped axle wagon known as "Kangeroo" while in Germany the kind of dropped axle wagon of the "Aachen" type and swop-bodies of the "Flexi-Van" type tend to be used. These latter types are currently being employed more and mo' often in all the countries. In this area, as well, statist should be improved in order to obtain better information on the development of the various techniques.In any case the Community should encourage the development of methods which allow simple and rapid trans- shipment with the minimum use of specialised rail vehicleseven more of specialised road vehicles in order to limit tf necessary investments to the strict minimum. 2.3. Instal lations (transshipment terminals)Table 4 (Annex II) gives a List of the main transshipment terminals (rail/road interchange) for combined carriage, i.e. about 60 such terminals of which half are in France and 16 in Germany. The creation of new terminals is being studied in Spain (Valencia and Barcelona ), in Italy ( Venice ), in France ( Morlaix and Noisy ), in the Netherlands (Grubbenvorst, Veendam, Flushing, Amsterdam) and in Belgium ( Courtrai ).INFLUENCE OF LIBERALIZATION MEASURES3.1. In order to provide information on the development ofcombined rail / road traffic and especially on the obstacles which might hinder its expansion , this report sets out,in Annex I , in a succinct manner , the opinions expressed by the representatives of the railways , own account and hire and reward road hauliers, users and the commercial combined carriage companies .These opinions reveal that there are still some anxieties of a commercial and of a psychological nature which might check the development of combined traffic but, in the Commission's view, these could be overcome in the light of the objective advantages which can follow for all those concerned in this new technique.Indeed, combined carriage uses rail for long distance journeys and is therefore capable of improving the conditions of rational operation. In particular block trains on well selected transport links constitute a form of traffic which is specifically adapted to the modern and profitable operation of the railways.On the other hand, carriage by rail over long distances allows road hauliers to reduce operating costs, especially in the area of labour which constitutes one of the most important elements of production costs, and to offer the customers a punctual servicewhich is not influenced by traffic or weather conditions.Consequently, the Commission is convinced, as has been proven by the effects in initiatives already adopted and which have been put in concrete form by the setting up of a joint rail/road Committee, that the initial difficulties can be overcome in the framework of increased co-operation between the two transport modes and by the adoption of adequate measures aimed at better guaranteeing their respective interests .The summary of observations in Annex I already allow certain factors whioh axe capable of playing a role in the political activities concerning this sector in the future to be brought out. -road hauliers : itspeed of carriage over long distances ;users : it brings rail carriage;the community: finally it brings a reduction in road traffic and , consequently , an increase in safety while at the sametime making a contribution towards protection of the environment .carried over longdistances ;-7-Finally, the Commission considers that the pilot-effectof the di active should be considered as a positive element , for theperiod in the immediate past and above all for the future development of tlvs traffic . This directive should be made oermarent as it aims at rait and road transport complementing one another and falls into line with those actions which take accountof the gr-neral interest and especially of the obligations of energy policy and regional development. In addition its extension to international carriage with third countries could be considered. The Commission even believes that it would be appropriate to study in greater depth the question of long distance national carriage with the aim that it should benefit from an analogous system.4. CONTINUATION OF THE ACTION AT NATIONAL AND COMMUNITY LEVELSA. 1 . General considerations on the desirabi lity of stimulating the development of combined rail/road carriageAt first sight , the " ferroutage" technique allows all interested parties to benefitthe railways: it allows them to bring in new traffic to bebrings advantages of safety , regularity together the advantages of door- to- door andThis ferroutage" technique implies close co-operation between the various transport modes both at investment level and at managementlevel. The narrow nature of the European land area tends to oblige most of this traffic to cross at least one frontier. Therefore it isnecessary to encourage close co-operation, on the one hand betweenthe various railway undertakings of the Community and on the other of the various road haulage undertakings both for hire and reward and own account , including also transport agents .The development of this technique therefore requires a dynamic investment policy at Community level, while at the same timeavoiding the simultaneous development of too many transport systems, and co-operation at management level by common actions in developing, stimulating and commercialising this kind of carriage.The public authorities who , generally speaking , are in favour of the development of combined transport in which they can see the benefits of economy of energy and the reduction of traffic on the mainroads, could encourage this development by certain positive measures as long as t-ley avoid the creation of distortions in the conditions of competition with classical transport modes .and -8■ 4.2 . Problems to be resolvedOn the basis of information at the Commission s disposal, the normal operation of the directive still comes up against the following difficulties in particular :4.2.1 . Authorization system for tug-units employed in terminal runsUnder the terms of Article 2 of the directive, combined carriage which comes under the criteria set out in the first article is freed from any quota or authorization system. However, Article 6 provides that national regulations concerning the conditions of admission to the profession and of access to the transport market shall not be altered . Thereby , vehicles used in combined carriage should, as in the past, be covered by national authorizations and come under national quotas insofar as such instruments are found in the national regulations of the various Member States .In "the light of information received "by the Commission, it seems that this situation could raise problems which rr.ust be elaborated from the point of view of the subsequent system; the following two questions are concerned :- the requirement that a tug unit belonging to a foreign company, stationed in a Member State for the purpose of effecting the terminal runs of its own semi-trailers, trailers or swop-bodies, should satisfy the national provisions of that Member State in­ sofar as quotas and authorizations are concerned;- the fact that the terminal runs of semi-trailers, trailers or swop-bodies used in own-account carriage are considered as if they were for hire and reward subject to authorization when the tug-units do not fulfil the conditions provided for own- account carriage .In order "thai; everything is done to stimulate comoinedrail/road transport, the Commission considers that more suitable solutions must be looked for .Whatever the circumstances the Commission is convinced of the fact that the development of combined carriage,boosted by all interested parties, risks being held back and possibly even blocked as long as some situations come under too bureaucratic a treatment . 4.?.2, Tariffs and rate fixingThe fixing of attractive rates is an important element which will decide the future of combined rail/road carriage.It is necessary to understand that the term "attractive" includes especially that the rates for carriage by rail should, on the one hand, prompt the road haulier to give up door-to-door carriage because of the greater costs involved and to choose combined carriage instead because of its less costly operation. On the other hand the rate should also be commercially acceptable to the railways.This last condition means that the revenues from combined carriage should, in the long run, allow the railwaysto cover the complete cost of this traffic. The question as to whether this is already the situation or could, in anycase, be the situation in the future, is a problem which deserves detailed study. Depending upon the results of this study, the question could be asked as to whether combined carriage by rail could be exempted from the requirement that it should be a commercial service, at least during a certain experimental period.In the context of this report this question can only be raised and not studied in depth. Above all the reply will depend on the degree of importance to be attributed to combined rail/road carriage within the framework of a transport policy based on the public interest.Apart from this question of transport rates the offer of a quality service, guaranteeing users both rapid and regular conveyance, is also a not unimportant factor capable of contributing towards the development of combined carriage.4*2.3. Determination of "appropriate nearest station"The Commission considers that it is necessary that the two criteria should bejudged separately for each transport service. They should, incidentally, be put forward in a cumulative way, in the sense that the "nearest" station from the point of view of the distance is not appropriate when, as much from the technical as from the commercial angle, it is not considered for optimum operation of such carriage. 4.2.5 .Rolling stock- 10 -Consequently, the Commission believes that it would be appropriate to prove flexibility in implementing this concept or to improve the present text of the directive in order to take adequate account of the practical transport requirements.4.2.4 . InfrastructureThe development of combined transport also depends on the possibilities for creating and modernising the rail/road trans- shipment centres. These centres should be well chosen in such away as to allow the establishment at Community level of a networkof complete trains which, by the ease of circulation they offer and the lowering of costs which result cannot fail to encourage combinedcarriage .The financial implications of the localisation of these transshipment centres can be very important. The multi-modal natureof these centres in fact requires that they should be surrounded by sufficient and fluid road routes .In this sector, financial action by the States and by the Community could be necessary in the form of subsidies fixed at a rate based on a proportion of the corresponding infrastructure costs and on the necessary equipment for the road share of the technique.Such actions should be planned together and carried out within the framework of an overall plan with an integrated view not only for "ferroutage" but also for the gantry cranes at the "trans- container" yards which could be common user on condition that payment is made for their use .Investments in rail rolling stock are usually made by the concerned . In France , nevertheless , it is the " Societerailwaysd'Equipement des Grands Itineraires " ( SEGI ) which buys the necessary special wagons. When this company was set up banks and builders of rolling stock provided capital and are therefore concerned in the development of combined transport.The SEGI draws up its orders on the basis of the needs expressed by NOVATRANS and hires out all its vehicle stock to that company for a length of time equivalent to the usual use and amortisation period of the wagons.In order to ensure the optimum adaptation of the vehicle stock to the needs at Community level one wonders whether it might not be worthwhile creating an international company on the lines "of the SEGI company .This company could progressively encourage greater uniformity of the too great diversity of "ferroutage" techniques which leads to poor profitability of the investments. < 1 )- 11 -In fact the multiplicity of techniques both on the railways sice with the different types of wagon and on the road s^de with the variety of semi-trailers or again the diversity of handling metliods lead to a wastaneof resources , especially at the international level .In conclusion it would be desirable for the hauliers concerned to work together towards defining uniform equipment .4.2.6 . Commercial organisationAn investigation into the possibilities of improving the organisation of combined transport is mainly the responsibility of the undertakings themselves .4.Z.6..1 . As far as railways are concerned the Commission has the impression , confirmed moreover by the experts , that an action based on more confidence and on a better understanding of the common interest will usefully contribute towards a development of this interesting traffic .The Commission has no criticisms to offer on any particular points. However it has highlighted a point which iscapable of being improved. It concerns its proposal aiming at mutual communication of the specific costs of carriage by complete trains in which some railway undertakings participate ( 1 ).The idea behind this suggestion, i.e. greater co-operation between the railway undertakings, could be developed further thanthe aspect of costs alone .4.2.6.2. As far as road hauliers and forwarding agents are concerned the creation of specialized companies for combined carr-'age has led to the solution of many organizational problems, andwithout doubt the most important ones. • During consultation between the Commission's services and the relevant sectors the questionwas asked as to whether an appeal would be useful when theopportunity offers , to the services of the " Bureau de rapprochement des entrepri ses" ( set up in the Commission ) in order to find a solution to the present or future problems concerning combined carriage .The Commission would merely put forward this idea. In cases where the governments also consider that this idea is worth taking into consideration there is nothing to stop this question being studied more deeply .Nevertheless , in the Commission 's view , problems of organization should be settled first of all by the undertakings themselves. This holds for the size of combined carriage under­ takings, the breadth of their field of activity, their commercial activities as well as "last but not least" their competitive policy (including the fairly delicate question of their behaviour vis a vis the companies for the transport of containers which are suosidiaries of the railway companies ).Article 6 of the proposed Council ( EEC) regulation concerning the fixing of uniform principles for the calculation of the cost : of railway undertakings <CJ N° C 155/10 of 2 July 1977) 5 .4*2.6.3. On the same lines it is worth mentioning also that the share of own account transport in combined carriage does not seem to have beensettled everywhere in a satisfactory way. Whatever the circumstances the own-account representatives complain of the fact that in some Member States their direct admission to combined carriage work is made difficultby exaggerated conditions in the sectors of fixing of rates and of organis­ ation , especially by making them work through transport agents .On the one hand one cainot criticise the railway undertakings for selling their combined carriage services at a greater cost to a single firm using combined carriage on own account than to major customers such as specialised combined carriage companies. These latter advance the argument that theyare responsible primarily for looking after the interests of their members. But, on the other hand, it does not seem justified to require the servicesof a transport agent every time.A solution could be found in fixing a rate which is economically justified and which does not allow any discrimination for own-account transport.In addition the greater the share of these latter in combined carriagethe greater the need to call upon the specialised combined carriage com­ panies , which will also provide them with economic advantages .CONCLUSIONS5-1 • The list of problems above is no doubt non-exhaustive . The Commission can only highlight those situations of which it has been in­ formed by the relevant economic sectors. It is not out of the question that the discussion of this report will reveal ether features to be in­ cluded or the need to make some corrections.Nevertheless it is worthwhile again drawing attention to the fact that the Commission , in accordance with its terms of reference , has refrained from submitting concrete proposals on the combined trans­ port .5.2 . The Commission , in accordance with sub-paragraph 2 of Article 7 of the directive , covered by this report , will submit a proposal during 1978 on the measures to be implemented in order to encourage the develop­ment of "ferroutage" which will replace the system set up under the present directive after 31 Deoember 1978*- 12 - Points of view expressed by the carriers and the users interested in combined carriageRailways' point of viewThe railway undertakings made the observation that the liberalisat- ion of combined carriage has had a positive influence on the behaviourof some road transport undertakings which have adapted their investment plans to the possibilities of combined carriage.On the other hand, they consider that the effect of this freedom could have been more favourable if the quotas for "pure" road transport, where they exist, had been stabilised or reduced. The railways state that there has been rather more a tendency towards increasing the quotas and that the greater freedom resulting from the directive has led to increased competition .The railway undertakings are in favour of measures which would tend to develop combined carriage more, even if this were combined with a revenue which was inferior to that obtained from other traffic. But they demand, in return, that this traffic should be deducted from road haulage and not from railway traffic which is carried out by other more profitable rail techniques.It is for this reason that they are in favour of an adjustment of the road transport quotas based on the activity recorded for combined carriage following its possible development. In this report the whole range of "pure road" transport activity and "combined transport" should be considered as road activities .The railways do not, through these demands, wish to interfere in the commercial management of the road hauliers.Point of view of the hire and reward road hauliersThe professional carriers of freight by road consider, on the other hand, that the directive is capable of distorting the conditions of com­ petition between the combined carriage technique and that of the classical carriage of freight by road. This influence would be especially strength­ ened if the directive and its objectives were used as a pretext for re­ fusing necessary alterations of the authorisation system for access tothe market in the road goods transport market.In addition the road hauliers fear that the railways could cancel the combined carriage services or discourage their development by alter­ ing the tariffs or by refusing to improve the organisation of the ser­ vices. Such action could affect their independence./•ANNEX I Despite these reservations hire and reward road hauliers are in favour of an extension of the directive on condition, however, that no connection is established "between the regulation and contract of combined carriage and that of road goods transport capacity, and that in this regard the promotion of combined carriage stays neutral.3. Point of view of own-account road hauliers and usersThe point of view of the own-account haulier is more or less the same. This transport sector is also opposed to the idea that combined carriageshould be used as an instrument "against" road haulage and "in favour"of the railways. It underlines especially the need to leave the commercial management of combined carriage to the road transport undertakings.This opinion is in accordance with the theme of the transport users which is also against any "artificial" co-ordination between railway androad and which considers that it would be as well , first of all , to leave the decision in the matter of future development of combined carriage to the market situation .4. Point of view of the commercial combined transport companiesThe member companies of U.I.R.R. (Union Internationale des trans­ ports combines rail/route) are in general positive as regards the directive. In particular they point out the reduction in the administrat­ ive structure and the removal of certain disadvantages such as the delays caused by the loss of authorisations, the time required for obtaining them and the refusal of loads because of unrenewed authorisations. Ingeneral these undertakings noted a greater flexibility in operations. In any case they are in favour of maintaining the present system even if only because of the brief length of the experimental period since 1 October 1975•ANNEX I Development of rail/road traffic Major international traffio links Wagons used for combined carriageMain depots (terminals) for coinbined carriage 1j {] I ISvrop bodiesNational InternationalTOTAL TRWSemi-trailers3 55 100 4 66 120 5 78 140 4 63 115 3 47 85 4 60 •108NCVATRANSHum­ Qross Index Num­ Cross Index dum­ Cross Index Num­ Cross Index Num­ Gros3 Index Num­■ Cross Index ber Tonnes ber Tonnes ber Tonnes ber Tonnes ber Tonnes berII Tonnes| HUPACi Sari-trallers .National123 100 6 100 21) 1836 (256 328 (354 65 International 0.51492087 S286 423328815 (655 533 103! Bruxelles, den 22. december 1977 KOMMISSIONENS MEDDELELSE TIL RÅDETBeretning om anvendelsen af Rådets direktiv af 17. februarom indførelse af fælles regler for visse former for kombi­ neret godstransport (jernbane/landevej) mellem medlemsstaterne(EFT nr. L 48 af 22.2.1975, s. 31/32)I henhold til ovennævnte direktivs artikel 7, stk. 1, skal Kommissionen inden den 31« december 1977 aflægge beretning til Råd.et om anvendelsen af denne foranstaltning og forelægge det forslag i forbindelse hermed.Medvedlagteberetningopfyldesdettekrav. Denindeholderderforførst og fremmest oplysninger om dette direktivs anvendelse i perioden fra1. oktober 1975 "til 1« juli 1977«Kommissionens tjenestegrene har i dette øjemed konsulteret følgende er­ hvervsorganisationer, der berøres af denne form for transport:- gruppen af de Ni1s jernbaneselskaber- de to forbindelsesudvalg (comités de liaison) i IRU (Union Interna­ tionale des Transports Routiers) for henholdsvis transport for fremmed og for egen regning- ved EP- L'Union Internationale des Transports Combines rail/route (U.I,R0R.)- UNTCE (Sammenslutningen af industri- og arbejdsgiverorganisationer i De europæiske Fællesskaber)® I beretningen belyses ovennævnte organisationers forskellige synspunkter, og der gøres opmærksom, på nogle problemer af mere teknisk art, som Kom­ missionen har fået kendskab til gennem de berørte kred3e i erhvervslivet.Kommissionen finder, at direktivets vejvisende virkning må betragtes som et positivt element i den fremtidige udvikling inden for denne trafik.Derfor kan Kommissionen allerede nu meddele, at den i henhold til direk­ tivets artikel 7» stk. 2, i 1978 vil forelægge Rådet forslag, som tager sigte på en permanent indførelse af den ordning, der blev indført på for- søgsbasis og den vil foreslå indførelse af de nødvendige foranstaltninger på baggrund af de indvundne erfaringer.Kommissionen finder imidlertid, at udviklingen af kombineret transport (jernbane/landevej på fællesskabsplan nødvendiggør en samlet politik,der går videre end til dette direktivs begrænsede formål, og som nød-, vendiggør en løsning på problemer på andre områder end adgangen til mar­ kedet, hvoraf nogle allerede er skitseret i denne beretning.Kommissionen regner i denne forbindelse med i løbet af 1978 også at frem­ sætte forslag, med henblik på at fremme udviklingen af kombineret trans­ port på fællesskabsplan. BERETNINGom anvendelsen af direktiv nr. 75/l30/SØFom indførelse af fælles regler Desuden har den internationale samhan­ del, som fra 1950 til begyndelsen af 1970'erne voksede støt med et årligt gennemsnit på ca. ffo - i den pågældende periode været påvirket af konjunkturnedgangen, og udviklingen af den transport , der varetages af kombinerede transportformer ,, er blevet midlertidigt "bremset.-2- E-3-Oplysningerne vedrørende udviklingen af kombineret transport (jorn'bcme/lendévej) »kal derfor vurderes på "baggrund af danne sitaution .2.2.2. Udviklingen i trafikken - Analyse af disse talPå grundlag af de statistiske oplysninger, der er indhentet hos de forskellige virksomheder, der beskæftiger sig med kom­ bineret transport, indeholder vedlagte tabel (bilag II. ta^- bel l) en oversigt over udviklingen siden 1971 i den transport (jernebane/landevej), der udføres i sættevogne, (herunder vogn­ tog) samt i vogne med udskifteligt lad.Til trods for at der er truffet sikkerhedsforanstaltninger har det ikke kunnet undgås at visse elementer er medregnet to gan­ge. Under forbehold heraf må det konstateres, at den samlede (nationale og internationale) bruttotrafik har udviklet sig således :1971 1972? ■–1 _ t- il 000 tons – 1973 1974 1975 1976 (1)Bruttotons |2981 3668!44524664 4301 5332 !iiIndeks100 123 149 I56144 179Af disse tal udgjorde den internationale trafik i 1976 ca. 1 million tons, altså ca. 19% af den samlede trafik.Det fremgår af disse tal, at den samlede trafik i 1976 er i betydelig fremgang efter at der i 1975 skete et fald i forhold til 1974.Med henblik på en placering af den trafik, der varetages af kombinerede transportformer (jernbane/landevej), i forhold til den samlede godstransport, ville det være forkert at sam­ menligne de samlede tal indbyrdes. For der tages ikke i dette til­fælde hensyn til, at kombineret transport (jernbane/landevej) kun kan udføres på rationel og rentabel måde over forholdsvis store afstande, på bestemte trafikforbindelser afhængigt af transportmængden samt for visse varekategorier. Skønt det er vanskeligt at . foretage et forsøg på sammenligning på dette grundlag som følge af mangel på objektive kriterier, ville gøre det muligt at bekræfte, at kombineret transport allerede på nuværende tidspunkt spiller en ikke ubetydelig og voksen­ de rolle på en række delmarkeder.Men der vil altid være visse grænser for udviklingen af denne fremgangsmåde hovedsagelig fordi den forudsætter transport af meget stor last (lastvogn eller sættevogne). Det er kun ud­ skifteligt lad, der er beslægtet med containeren, som ikke har denne ulempe.Ikkedestomindreerdentransport, somudføresafvirksomhe­ der, der beskæftiger sig med kombineret transport inden for Fællesskabet stærkt stigende (+ 22% i 1. halvår af 1977)«2.2.3« Bidrag til denne trafik fra de forskellige virksomheder, der beskæftiger sig med kombineret transport'Den kombinerede transport, (jernbane/landevej), som kaldes "piggy-back"–transport udføres af virksomheder, der har datter­ selskaber i nogle europæiske lande.. I Forbundsrepublikken Tyskland blev 20% af den internatio­ nale transport i 1975 udført af KOMBIVERKEHR,. I Belgien blev 9% denne transport udført af T.R.W. ,. I Franrkig blev Afrfo af denne trafik udført af UOVATRAKS,. I Italien blev 2% af denne trafik udført af FERPAC,. I Nederlandene blev, 10% af denne trafik udført af TRAILSTAR, . I Schweiz blev 15% af denne trafik udført af HUPAC.Siden 1970 hs-r disse selskaber været sluttet sammen med et syvende, A.S.G.(Sverige) i 1'Union Internationale des trans­ ports combinés rail/route (UIRR). 2.2.4 .2.2.5 . •Desuden er der "blevet nedsat et blandet udvalg (jerribane/lan- aevej ) Tjaot&and® af da esoislfftbar , der ar me&leramer af UlHfl egjernbanerne i medlemsstaterne , Schweiz og Østrig , med det for­ mål at koordinere bestræbelserne på internationalt plan med henblik på udviklingen af transporten (jerribane/landevej).Trafikkens fordeling efter trafikforbindelserI tabellen (bilag II, tabel 2) anføres de vigtigste interna­ tionale forbindelser , der berøres af denne trafik . Fordeling efter metoder til kombineret transportVirksomheder , der beskæftiger sig med kombineret transport , anvender forskellige metoder til "piggy-back"-transport . Der kan skelnes mellen to store kategorier:- de metoder, hvorved vognen tilpasses køretøjet (unaersænkede vogne eller vogne med styreskinner):- de metoder, hvor køretøjet er udformet på en sådan måde, at det køn tilpasses vognen (særlige sættevogne eller vogne med udskifteligt lad).Det har ikke været muligt at angive en fordeling af trafikken efter de forskellige anvendte metoder . Det kan kun angives , at JTOVATRANS i Frankrig i større udstrækning anvender den så­ kaldte "kænguru"~metode med undersænket vogn med rum, mens det snarere er metoden med undersænket vogn af Aachen-typen og vogne med udskifteligt lad af Flexi-Van-typen der anvendes i Tyskland, de sidstnævnte gennemgår for øjeblikket en hastigudvikling i alle lande. Også på dette område burde den stati­ stiske plan gøres mere detaljeret med henblik på at indhente bedre oplysninger om udviklingen af de forskellige metoder.Fællesskabet burde under alle omstændigheder begunstige udvik­ lingen af metoder, som muliggør en enkelt og hurtig omladning med mindst mulig specialisering af vogne, der anvendes til transport med jernbane og ad landevej , idet der gøres bestræ­belser på at begrænse de nødvendige investeringer til et mini­ mum . 3 .VIRKNINGER AF LIBERALISERINGSFORANSTALTNINGERNE3.1. Med henblik på at foretage nogle vurderinger af udviklingen i den kombinerede transport (jernbane/landevej) og navnlig af hindringerne for udviklingen af den, indeholder denne rapport i bilag I en kort­ fattet redegørelse for de opfattelser, som repræsentanterne for jern­ banerne , de virksomheder , der udfører transport ad landevej for egen og fremmed regning , brugerne og de virksomheder , der udfører kombi­ neret transport , har givet udtryk for desangående .Disse opfattelser viser, at der endnu er visse betænkeligheder af han­ delsmæssig eller psykologisk art, som kan bremse udviklingen af kom­ bineret transport , men Kommissionen finder , at disse bør kunne over­ vindes på baggrund af de objektive fordele, som denne nye metode kan medføre for alle berørte parter.For ved kombineret transport anvendes jernbanen over lange stræknin­ ger , og der kan drages, fordel af betingelserne for rationel drift .Navnlig transporten i blokvognstog og på udvalgte forbindelser er for så vidt angår jernbaner særlig velegnet til moderne og rentabel drift .På den anden side gør transport med jernbane over lange strækninger det muligt for virksomheder, der beskæftiger sig med transport ad landevej at nedbringe de driftsudgifter, navnlig med hensyn til ar­ bejdskraft, som er en af de vigtigste bestanddele af kostprisen og at yde kunderne en tjeneste , der er kendetegnet ved sin præcision , da den ikke påvirkes af trafik- eller vejrforhold.Som det er bevist gennem virkningerne af de initiativer , der allere­ de er vedtaget, og som er konkretiseret i oprettelse af et blandet udvalg (transport med jernbane/ad landevej) er Kommissionen overbe­ vist om at vanskelighederne i begyndelsen vil kunne overvindes i for­ bindelse med et mere intensivt samarbejde mellem de to transportfor­ mer og ved gennemførelse af tilstrækkelige foranstaltninger, der sig­ ter mod en bedre opfyldelse af deres respektive interesser.De synspunkter, der er anført i bilag I, gør det allerede nu muligt at uddrage visse elementer, som kan få betydning i fremtiden for de politiske aktiviteter på dette område.2.3 «Anlæg ( oplagspladser )Tabellen (bilag II, tabel 4) indeholder en liste over de vigtigste oplagspladser for kombineret transport (jernbane/landevej), dvs. om­ kring 60 oplagspladser, af hvilke halvdelen er beliggende i Frankrig og 16 i Tyskland. Oprettelsen af nye oplagspladser er ved at blive ■undersøgt i Spanien (Valencia og Barcelona), i Italien (Venezia), i Frankrig (Morlaix og Noisy), i Nederlandene (Grubbenvorst, Veendam, Vlissingen, Amsterdam) og i Belgien (Courtrai).-6- -7-Det må konkluderes, at Kommissionen finder direktivets virkning som forsøg skal "betragtes som et positivt element ikke "blot for den forløbne periode men også for den fremtidige udvikling inden for denne trafik. Dette direk­ tiv, som medfører komplementaritet inden for transport med jernbane og ad landevej, og som er i overensstemmelse med de handlinger, der sigter modat tage hensyn til samfundets interesse , og de forpligtelser , som navnlighidrører fra energi- og egnsudviklingspolitikken , "permanent. Desuden skal det planlægges at udvide det til også at omfatte den internationale transport med tredjelande. Kommissionen finder endog,at spørgsmålet om national transport , der udføres over stor afstand , bør uddybes med henblik på at denne kan drage fordel af en tilsvarende ordning.4. FORTSÆTTELSE AF HANDLINGEN-NATIONALT OG PÅ FÆLLESSKABSPLAN■ 4.1 . Generelle betragtninger vedrørende muligheden for at fremme kombineret transport ( jernbane/landevej )Det karakteristiske- ved "piggy-back"-metoden er ved en overfladisk betragt­ ning, at den er til fordel for alle de berørte parter.- Den gør det muligt for jernbanerne at varetage den nye transport, der udføres over lange strækninger.- For virksomheder , der er beskæftiget med transport ad landevej , frembyder den fordele med hensyn til sikker, regelmæssig og hurtig transport over lange strækninger.- For brugerne frembyder den fordele både fra transporten ad landevej fra dør til dør og transporten med jernbane.- For samfundet betyder den endelig en lettelse af landevejstrafikken og som følge heraf en øget sikkerhed samtidig med at den indgår parallelt i en aktion vedrørende miljøbeskyttelse.Men denne "piggy-back"-metode indebarer både med hensyn til investeringer . og forvaltning et nært samarbejde mellem de forskellige transportformer. Men på grund af det europæiske områdes ringe udstrækning, må de fleste af disse transporter føres over mindst én grænse. Der må således fremmes et nært samarbejde dels mellem de forskellige jernbanevirksomheder inden for Fællesskabet dels med de forskellige virksomheder, der er beskæftiget med transport ad landevej for egen og fremmed regning herunder ligeledes hjæl- petjenester i forbindelse med transport.Udviklingen af denne metode kræver således, at der på fællesskabsplan føres en dynamisk investeringspolitik samtidig med at det undgås at udvikle alt for mange forskellige transportsystemer samtidigt samt at der foretages et forvaltningsmæssigt samarbejde med hensyn til fælles aktioner inden for fremme og udførelse af denne transport.De offentlige myndigheder, som i almindelighed er positivt indstillet over for udviklingen af kombineret transport, hvori de ser en energibesparende faktor samt et middel til aflastning af landevejstrafikken, ville kunne anspore til denne udvikling gennem visse positive foranstaltninger, på den betingelse at de undgår at skabe forvridninger i konkurrencevilkårene over for de klassiske transportformer.'bør derfor opretholdes -8-4.2. Problemer, der, skal løsesIfølge oplysninger som Kommissionen råder over, hæmmes den normale gennem­ førelse af direktivet af nedenstående vanskeligheder:4.2.1. Bemyndigelsesordning for "befordring over terminalstrækningerI henhold til artikel 2 i direktivet, opfylder kombineret transport de i artikel 1 fastsatte kriterier og fritages for enhver ordning med. kontin­ genter og "bemyndigelse. I henhold til artikel 6 foretages der dog ingen ændring af de nationale "bestemmelser vedrørende "betingelserne for adgang til erhvervet som fragtfører og til transportmarkedet. Derfor skal de kø­ retøjer, der anvendes inden for kombineret transport, ligesom tidligere, omfattes af nationale "bemyndigelser og undergives nationale kontingenter,"bestemmel­Af oplysninger indhentet af Kommissionen fremgår det , at denne situation kan rejse problemer, der skal undersøges på grundlag af en yderligere ord­ ning; det drejer sig om følgende to spørgsmål:- kravet om at en traktor, der tilhører en udenlandsk virksomhed, og som er anbragt i en medlemsstat med henblik på at varetage terminaltranspor­ ten med denne medlemsstats egne sættevogne, påhængsvogne eller vogne med udskifteligt lad skal opfylde denne medlemsstats nationale bestemmelser for så vidt angår kontingenter og bemyndigelse;– den omstændighed, at terminaltransport med sættevogne, påhængsvogne og disses løse overbygninger, der anvendes til transport for egen regning, anses for erhvervsmæssig transport og undergives bemyndigelse, når trak­ torerne ikke opfylder de betingelser, der er fastsat for transport for egen regning.Ked henblik på at træffe alle nødvendige foranstaltninger for at fremme kombineret transport (jernbane/landevej) finder Kommissionen, at der bør findes mere hensigtsmæssige løsninger.Under alle omstændigheder er Kommissionen overbevist om, at udviklingen af kombineret transport , over for hvilken alle interesserede kredse har en positiv holdning, risikerer at blive forsinket og eventuelt bremset så længe der foretages en alt for bureaukratisk behandling af visse forhold.såfremt disse findes i de forskellige medlemsstaters nationale ser . -9-4.2.2 . Tariffer og prisdannelseEn fordelagtig prisdannelse er en betydelig faktor, som vil afgøre fremti­den for kombineret transport (jernbane/landevej). Ved "fordelagtig" for­ stås, at specielt prisen for transport med jernbane skal bevirke, at virk­somheder, der udfører transport ad landevej, anspores til ikke at udføre transport ad landevej fra afsenderen til modtageren men i stedet vælge kom­ bineret transport, som ville sikre en billigere drift. På den anden side skal denne transportpris ligeledes være forretningsmæssig acceptabel for jernbanerne .Sidstnævnte betingelse ville betyde, at indtægterne fra kombineret trans­ port på lang sigt ville kunne gøre det muligt for jernbanerne at dække om­kostningerne fuldt ud i forbindelse med denne transport. Hvorvidt dette allerede er tilfældet for øjeblikket eller vil kunne gennemføres under al­ le omstændigheder i fremtiden , er et problem , som må undersøges nøjere . I­ følge resultaterne af denne undersøgelse opstår spørgsmålet om, hvorvidt man ikke, i det mindste for en vis forsøgsperiode, burde undlade at betrag­ te den kombinerede transport med jernbaner som udført i kommercielt øjemed.Uafhængigt af dette spørgsmål om transportprisen er tilbudet om en kvali­ tetsmæssig service, som ville sikre brugerne en hurtig og regelmæssig trans­ port ligeledes en ikke ubetydelig faktor, som kan bidrage til udviklingenaf kombineret transport.4.2.3 . Bestemmelse af den "hensigtsmæssige og nærmeste banegård "Kommissionen anser det for nødvendigt , at de to kriterier , den "hensigts­ mæssige" og den "nærmeste" banegård vurderes for hver enkelt transport- ydelse. De må i øvrigt være til stede samtidigt, i den forstand at den"nærmeste" banegård ikke er "hensigtsmæssig", når den ikke indgår i over­ vejelserne om den optimale udførelse af en sådan transport set ud fra både et teknisk og forretningsmæssigt synspunkt.I forbindelse med denne beretning kan dette spørgsmål kun rejses og ikke uddybes. Svaret vil først og fremmest afhænge af den betydning, som kombi­neret transport (jernbane/landevej) tillægges i forbindelse med en portpolitik, der sigter mod den kollektive interesse..trans- - 10 -Kommissionen, finder derfor , at det ville være hensigtsmæssigt » om der vi­ ses smidighed ved attvendel&en af dette Taa.sre'b, elle? at d&p fstetRøes en ændring af det nuværende direktiv med henblik på tilstrækkelig hensyntagen til de praktiske krav i forbindelse med transport.4.2.4 « InfrastrukturUdviklingen af kombineret transport er ligeledes afhængig af mulighederne for oprettelse og modernisering af centre for omladning i forbindelse med transport med jernbane/ad landevej. Disse centre bør vælges fornuftigt, så­ ledes at de kan gøre det muligt på fællesskabsplan at oprette et komplet vogntogsne.t , som på . grund af de lettelser i trafikken , det vil medføre , og det fald i omkostningerne, der vil være en følge deraf, ikke kunne undgåat fremme udviklingen af kombineret transport.Anbringelsen af disse centre for omladning er et spørgsmål hvis finansiel­ le følgevirkninger kan være betydningsfulde. Da disse centre kan anvendes ved flere transportformer, må de nødvendigvis omgives af tilstrækkelige forbindelsesveje .På dette område ville finansieringen ske i form af tilskud fra. staterne og fra Fællesskabet for en endnu ikke fastsat del af omkostningerne, som svarer til den infrastruktur og det udstyr, der er nødvendigt for den del af metoden, der vedrører transport ad landevej.Lignende aktioner bør udtænkes i fællesskab og gennemføres i forbindelse med en samlet planlægning og en integreret holdning ikke blot med hensyn til "piggy-back"~transport men også med hensyn til overdækkede gårde på pladserne for "transcontainere", som ville kunne anvendes i fællesskab mod betaling af en brugsafgift.4.2.5 . Rullende materielInvesteringerne i rullende materiel til jernbaner foretages normalt af de berørte jernbaner .I Frankrig er det imidlertid Société d'Equipement des Grands Itinéraires(SEGl), som har tilrettelsen af dette selskab blev der anmodet om deltagelse fra banker og virksomheder, beskæftiget med konstruktion af materiel i forbindelse med transport ad landevej, som således er interesseret i udviklingen af kombi­ neret transport.SEGI udarbejder sine ordreprogrammer efter de behov, som NOVATRANS har gi­ vet udtryk for, og udlejer hele sin park til dette selskab for en periode, der mindst svarer til den normale periode for afskrivning og anvendelse af vogne .Med henblik på en optimal tilpasning af vognparken til behovene på fælles- skabsplan , opstår det spørgsmål , om det ikke ville være hensigtsmæssigt atplanlægge oprettelse af et internationalt selskab efter samme mønster som SEGI .Dette selskab ville gradvis kunne fremme en ensartethed i den alt for sto­ re forskelligartethed i "piggy-back"-metoderne, som medfører en dårlig forrentning af investeringerne..opgave at erhverve de nødvendige specialvogne. Ved op­ - 11De mangfoldige metoder både inden for -transport med jernbane på grund afda forskellige vogntyper og inden for transport ad laM&vøj på grund af de forskellige sættevogne eller de forskellige metoder til godshåndtering med­ fører ressourcespild først og fremmest på internationalt plan.Det må konkluderes , at det ville være ønskeligt , om de berørte transport­ virksomheder i fællesskab fastsætter ensartet materiel.4.2.6. Handelsmæssig organisationUndersøgelse af mulighederne for en bedre organisation af kombineret trans­ port henhører først og fremmest under virksomhederne.4.2.6.1, For så vidt angår '.jernbanerne er det Kommissionens indtryk, hvil­ ket i øvrigt er bekræftet af eksperterne, at handling baseret på en større tillid og større forståelse af de falles interesser ville være et gavnligt bidrag til udviklingen af denne berørte trafik.Kommissionen har ingen kritik at fremsætte på bestemte konkrete punkter. Den har dog understreget et punkt, der kan forbedres. Det drejer sig orn dens forslag vedrørende den gensidige meddelelse om de særlige omkostnin­ ger inden for transport ped komplette vogntog, i hvilke visse jernbaner deltager (l ).Den idé, der ligger til grund for dette forslag, nemlig et øget samarbejde mellem jernbanerne, ville kunne generaliseres ud over det egentlige omkost- ningsaspekt .4.2.6.2 , For så vidt angår virksomheder , der udfører transport ad landevej , samt speditører har oprettelse af særlige selskaber inden for kombineret transport gjort det muligt at løse talrige og utvivlsomt de vigtigste pro­ blemer vedrørende organisation. Under konsultation mellem de berørte kred­ se og Kommissionens tjenestegrene opstod det spørgsmål, om det ikke ville være hensigtsmæssigt ved denne lejlighed at rette henvendelse til "Konto­ ret for Virksomhedssamarbejde ", som er oprettet ved Kommissionen , med hen­ blik på løsningen af de nuværende eller fremtidige problemer i forbindelsemed kombineret transport.Kommissionen nøjes med at fremsætte dette synspunkt. Såfremt regeringerne ligeledes finder, at det må tages under overvejelse, er der intet til hin­ der for en tilbundsgående undersøgelse af dette spørgsmål«Efter Kommissionens mening må problemerne vedrørende organisation dog først og fremmest løses af virksomhederne selv. Dette er værdifuldt for størrel­ sen af de virksomheder, der beskæftiger sig med kombineret transport, ud­ strækningen af deres virkeområde , deres handelsmæssige aktiviteter , og sidst men ikke mindst deres konkurrencepolitik (herunder det meget ømtålelige spørgsmål vedrørende deres adfærd over for jernbanernes datterselskaber in­ den for containertransport).4.2.6.3 , I denne forbindelse bør det ligeledes understreges , at deltagelse af transportvirksomheder , der udfører transport 'for' egen regning , i kombi­ neret transport ikke gynes.at være afklaret på tilfredsstillende måde over­ alt. Under alle omstændigheder klager repræsentanterne for transport udført(l) Artikel 6 i Rådets forordning (EØF) om fastsættelse af ensartede prin­ cipper for jernbanevirksomheders omkostningsberegning (ÉFTf nr. C 155 af 2. juli 1977. s. 10). - 12 -for egen regning over, at deres direkte adgang til kombineret transport i visse medlemsstater vanskeliggøres af fot strenge betingelser inden for prisdannelse og organisation, navnlig ved at det pålægges dem at henvende sig til speditører.På den ene side kan det ikke bebrejdes jernbanerne at de forlanger mere for deres tjenester inden for kombineret transport hos en virksomhed, derudfører kombineret transport for egen regning end hos. store kunder, som f.eks. selskaber, der er specialiserede inden for kombineret transport. Sidstnævntefremsætter på deres side det argument, at de først og fremmest skal varetage deres medlemmers interesser. Men på den anden side synes det ikke begrundet, at der under alle omstændigheder kræves medvirken af en speditør.Der ville kunne findes en løsning i en økonomisk berettiget prisdannelse, som ikke medfører forskelsbehandling over for virksomheder, der udfører transport for egen regning. Desuden ville en stærkere deltagelse fra sidst­ nævntes side i kombineret transport, ved medvirken af selskaber, der er specialiseret i kombineret transport, ligeledes frembyde økonomiske forde­ le for disse.5. KONKLUSION5.1. Ovennævnte opregning af problemerne er sikkert ikke udtømmende. Kommissio­ nen kan kun beskrive de forhold, som den har fået kendskab til gennem de berør­ te kredse i erhvervslivet. Det udelukkes ikke, at drøftelsen af denne beretning fremkalder andre elementer, som skal medtages, eller påviser nødvendigheden af at foretage visse ændringer i den.Opmærksomheden må derfor endnu en gang henledes på, at Kommissionen i overens­ stemmelse med den opgave, der er pålagt den, har afholdt sig fra at forelægge Rådet konkrete forslag vedrørende kombineret transport.5.2. I henhold til artikel 7» stk. 2, i det direktiv, der er omhandlet i denne beretning, vil Kommissionen i løbet af 1978 fremsætte et forslag vedrørende de foranstaltninger, der skal iværksættes med henblik på at fremme udviklingen af "piggy-back", og som efter den 31« december 1978 skal erstatte den nuværende ordning, der er indført ved det nævnte direktiv. Synspunkter, fremført af de transportvirksomheder og "brugere, der "berøres af kembineret transport*Synspunkt , fremført af jern DanerneJernbanevirksomhederne gør opmærksom på, at liberaliseringen af kombineret transport har haft en positiv indflydelse på den holdning, der udvises af visse virksomheder, som udfører transport ad landevej, og som har tilpas­ set deres investeringsplaner til mulighederne for kombineret transport.Derimod mener de, at liberaliseringen kunne have haft en mere positiv virk­ning, hvis kontingenterne for "ren" landevejstransport - hvor sådanne fin­ des - var blevet stabiliseret eller reduceret. Jernbanerne konstaterer sna­ rere en tendens til udvidelse af kontingenterne, samt at den liberalise­ ring, der følger af direktivet, har givet anledning til en øget konkurren­ce.Jernbanevirksomhederne er , positivt stemt over for foranstaltninger, der skal udvikle kombineret transport yderligere , selv med en indtægt , der er klart lavere end den, de opnår ved anden transport. Men de kræver til gen-' gæld, at denne form for transport bliver afskrevet på landevejstransportog ikke på jernbanetransport, der foretages med andre og mere rentable me­ toder.Derfor udtaler jernbanerne sig til fordel for en regulering af kontingen­ terne for landevejstransport i forhold til den aktivitet, der konstateres med hensyn til kombineret transport , efterhånden som denne sidstnævnte form for transport eventuelt udvikles, idet den samlede transport "udelukkende ad landevej" og "kombineret" må betragtes som en aktivitet inden for trans­ port ad landevej.Jernbanerne vil med disse krav ingenlunde anfægte den handelsmæssige kontrol, som de virksomheder , der udfører landevejstransport , sidder inde med .Synspunkt, fremført af virksomheder, der udfører transport for fremmed regningDe virksomheder , der udfører erhvervsmæssig godstransport ad landevej , me­ ner derimod, at direktivet kan forvanske konkurrencevilkårene mellem den kombinerede transport og den klassiske godstransport ad landevej. Denne virkning ville især blive forstærket, hvis direktivet og de deri tilstræb­ te mål blev anvendt som påskud til at afvise de nødvendige tilpasninger af bemyndigelsesordningerne vedrørende adgang til markedet for godstransport ad landevej.Desuden frygter de virksomheder , der udfører transport ad landevej , at jern­ banerne skal ophæve de kombinerede transporttjenester eller modarbejde ud­ viklinger^ heraf ved ændring af tarifferne eller ved at afvise en bedre or­ ganisering af disse transporttjenester, hvilket kunne påvirke deres uafhæn­ gighed .De virksomheder , der udfører transport ad landevej for fremmed regning , er- klarer sig trods disse forbehold positivt indstillet med hensyn til at for­BILAG I - 2 - BILAG Ilænge direktivet, dog pa den "betingelse, at der ikke oprettes nogen for­ bindole« mallem bestemmelserne for kombineret transport og reguleringen af kapaciteten for godstransport ad landevej, og at fremstødet for kombi­ neret transport fortsat er neutralt i den forbindelse.3. Synspunkt, fremført af virksomheder, der udfører transport for egen regning , og af brugereDe virksomheder, der udfører transport for egen regning, har tilnærmelses­ vis fremført det samme synspunkt. Denne transportsektor er ligeledes mod­ stander af, at kombineret transport anvendes som et middel "mod" transport ad landevej og "til fordel for" transport med jernbane. Den understreger især nødvendigheden af, at kontrollen med kombineret transport overlades til de virksomheder , der udfører transport ad landevej .Denne mening falder sammen med transportbrugernes teori, hvori disse ud­ trykker deres modstand mod enhver "kunstig" koordinering af transport med jernbane og transport ad landevej , og de mener ligeledes , at den fremtidi­ ge udvikling af kombineret transport må afgøres af situationen på markeder­ ne.4. Synspunkt, fremført af de handelsselskaber, der udfører kombineret transportDe selskaber, der er medlemmer af UIRR (Union internationale des trans­ ports combinés rail/route) er generelt positivt stemt over for direktivet. De gør især opmærksom på lettelsen af den administrative struktur og bort­ fald af visse ulemper, såsom de forsinkelser, der opstår ved tab af tilla­ delser, den tid, der medgår til opnåelse af nye tilladelser samt nægtelse af lastning , når tilladelserne ikke er blevet fornyet . Generelt har disse virksomheder konstateret en større smidighed i driften. De erklærer sig i alle tilfælde positivt indstillet over for en bibeholdelse af det nuværen­ de system, om ikke for andet, så på grund af den korte forsøgsperiode fra, den 1 . oktober 1975 « Tabel 1 2 34 .•STATISTIKKER iUdvikling af transporten (jernbane/landevej)De vigtigste internationale forbindelserVogne, der anvendes til kombineret transportDe vigtigst^ oplagspladser i forbindelse uied kombineret transport . • . 1» SBSSatBSS3SSS:8S3C3SSaSGBI5&tSSSeC5SBILAG II !NationalInternational III 18II1.458 100*62 100 ml?.D 100πNOVATRMS EXM– Scmi-'tr£;il crs *berj Index iSvrop bodies Nationalînt ernational TOTALTRW Serai-trail erss»I !■1 !(Total) IInternationalI TRAILSTAR-I Semi-trailers ^(Total)I InternationalI HPPAGI Sgaij^gdlersI St-rop baclies46I I6 1566 1266 (256 33ΓΠπ πΓΊΡΊmπ Π1Internationalr 23National100 6 100 25 International 0.5 D208(3542881510(655 533 s655 533! .Tonnes16 327ber Tannesber Tonnes120 22 482ber Tonnesber Tonnes berI TonnesÏÏÔ 1778 6 π233 8 6136 I ι IIIιI;) 1231971 I1r– –Index I100!I 393147 24514 157 18380 116 23 500 153Development of rail/road combined carriage since 1971 Table 1in semi-trailers (including vehicle combinations) ana swop bodies of 12m and 2 x 7m (indices calculated in relation to 1971).~1972 !
